The long/short was that Michael L. was at my home within 2 hours and after asking me a few questions immediately zeroed in on the problem which was a faulty outlet plug that had blown. <review>We live in Orem and this is the place we bring our Pets. Perhaps it's because they are located in a more affluent area that is more likely to have pets that are treated as members of the household, I don't know. I do know that while things can seem a bit busy and perfunctory at times, they have staff and doctors that care. We brought our recent Affenpinscher puppy purchase to get his first checkout. He'll never know another place. The doctor we had was enthralled with his personality and asked to make sure we come to him in the future.
We brought our previous rescue rat terrier here for 15 years, and our Golden Lab here at the end of her life when we wanted a vet we preferred over our local options. We've been coming for a long time.
We brought our cats over the years. We even had an Abyssinian that had to have an eye removed and ear amputated because of cancer. They've been great with all of them. They may not be the cheapest option around town, but the prices are fair for what they provide.</review>< user_id>
